],\n  \"text\": \"Django's URL routing system is implemented across multiple modules in the django/urls package and django/conf/urls package. The core files are:\\n\\n1. **django/urls/conf.py** - Provides the main URL configuration functions:\\n   - `include(arg, namespace=None)`: Includes another URL configuration, supporting tuples for namespace hints and app_name specification.\\n   - `path(route, view, kwargs=None, name=None)`: Modern path-based URL pattern using RoutePattern (replaces the deprecated Django 1.x url() function).\\n   - `re_path(route, view, kwargs=None, name=None)`: Regex-based URL pattern using RegexPattern (also replaces deprecated url()).\\n   - `_path()`: Internal function that both path() and re_path() are built from using functools.partial.\\n\\n2. **django/urls/resolvers.py** - Contains the URL dispatcher classes:\\n   - `URLResolver`: Main dispatcher class that resolves URLs to view callbacks, manages urlpatterns, and handles URL reversal. Has resolve() method for matching paths and _reverse_with_prefix() for URL reversal.\\n   - `URLPattern`: Represents a single URL pattern with a pattern object, callback view, default arguments, and name. Has resolve() method for matching.\\n   - `ResolverMatch`: Result object returned by URL resolution containing the matched view, args, kwargs, url_name, namespaces, and route information.\\n   - `RegexPattern`: Pattern class for regex-based URL patterns with LocaleRegexDescriptor for language-specific compilation.\\n   - `RoutePattern`: Pattern class for modern route-based URL patterns with converter support and LocaleRegexRouteDescriptor.\\n   - `LocalePrefixPattern`: Special pattern for i18n language prefix patterns.\\n   - `get_resolver(urlconf=None)`: Gets or creates a URLResolver instance with caching.\\n   - `get_ns_resolver()`: Creates namespaced resolver for captured parameters in parent URLconf.\\n   - `_route_to_regex()`: Converts path() style routes to regex patterns, handling converters like <int:id>, <slug:name>, etc.\\n\\n3. **django/urls/base.py** - High-level URL routing API:\\n   - `resolve(path, urlconf=None)`: Entry point that resolves a URL path to a ResolverMatch object.\\n   - `reverse(viewname, urlconf=None, args=None, kwargs=None, current_app=None, query=None, fragment=None)`: Reverses a URL from a view name/path.\\n   - `reverse_lazy()`: Lazy version of reverse().\\n   - `is_valid_path()`: Convenience method to check if a path is valid.\\n   - `translate_url()`: Translates URLs for i18n.\\n   - `get_urlconf()`, `set_urlconf()`: Thread/task-local URLconf management.\\n   - `get_script_prefix()`, `set_script_prefix()`, `clear_script_prefix()`: SCRIPT_NAME prefix management.\\n   - `clear_url_caches()`: Clears cached resolvers and callables.\\n\\n4. **django/urls/converters.py** - Path converters for route parameters:\\n   - `IntConverter`, `StringConverter`, `UUIDConverter`, `SlugConverter`, `PathConverter`: Built-in converters for path() parameters.\\n   - `register_converter()`: Register custom converters.\\n   - `get_converters()`: Returns all available converters.\\n\\n5. **django/urls/utils.py** - Utility functions:\\n   - `get_callable(lookup_view)`: Resolves string view paths to callable functions.\\n   - `get_mod_func()`: Splits dotted paths into module and function parts.\\n\\n6. **django/urls/exceptions.py** - Exception classes:\\n   - `Resolver404`: Raised when URL resolution fails.\\n   - `NoReverseMatch`: Raised when URL reversal fails.\\n\\n7. **django/conf/urls/__init__.py** - Exports include and default error handlers.\\n\\n8. **django/conf/urls/i18n.py** - Internationalization support:\\n   - `i18n_patterns(*urls, prefix_default_language=True)`: Wraps URL patterns with language prefix.\\n   - `is_language_prefix_patterns_used()`: Detects if i18n_patterns is used.\\n\\n9. **django/conf/urls/static.py** - Debug static file serving:\\n   - `static(prefix, view=serve, **kwargs)`: Helper for serving media files in debug mode.\\n\\n10. **django/urls/__init__.py** - Main package that exports all public APIs.\\n\\n**Historical Note on patterns() function**: The `patterns()` function (used in Django versions before 1.10) has been removed and replaced with direct list-based urlpatterns. In the current codebase, URL patterns are defined as simple Python lists containing URLPattern and URLResolver objects created via path(), re_path(), and include() calls. The urlpatterns attribute is accessed and processed by include() and URLResolver.url_patterns property.\\n\\nThe current URL routing architecture processes both legacy patterns (through urlpatterns lists) and the modern routing through the common URLResolver, URLPattern, RegexPattern, and RoutePattern classes, with path converters providing type-safe parameter extraction.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":10,"cache_creation_input_tokens":378,"cache_read_input_tokens":48764,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":378},"output_tokens":3,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"70affa15-35c3-410f-89dd-40f64d4b262f","uuid":"9deea157-cac6-488a-bdf0-dee198ec3d01"}

The core files are:\\n\\n1. **django/urls/conf.py** - Provides the main URL configuration functions:\\n   - `include(arg, namespace=None)`: Includes another URL configuration, supporting tuples for namespace hints and app_name specification.\\n   - `path(route, view, kwargs=None, name=None)`: Modern path-based URL pattern using RoutePattern (replaces the deprecated Django 1.x url() function).\\n   - `re_path(route, view, kwargs=None, name=None)`: Regex-based URL pattern using RegexPattern (also replaces deprecated url()).\\n   - `_path()`: Internal function that both path() and re_path() are built from using functools.partial.\\n\\n2. **django/urls/resolvers.py** - Contains the URL dispatcher classes:\\n   - `URLResolver`: Main dispatcher class that resolves URLs to view callbacks, manages urlpatterns, and handles URL reversal. Has resolve() method for matching paths and _reverse_with_prefix() for URL reversal.\\n   - `URLPattern`: Represents a single URL pattern with a pattern object, callback view, default arguments, and name. Has resolve() method for matching.\\n   - `ResolverMatch`: Result object returned by URL resolution containing the matched view, args, kwargs, url_name, namespaces, and route information.\\n   - `RegexPattern`: Pattern class for regex-based URL patterns with LocaleRegexDescriptor for language-specific compilation.\\n   - `RoutePattern`: Pattern class for modern route-based URL patterns with converter support and LocaleRegexRouteDescriptor.\\n   - `LocalePrefixPattern`: Special pattern for i18n language prefix patterns.\\n   - `get_resolver(urlconf=None)`: Gets or creates a URLResolver instance with caching.\\n   - `get_ns_resolver()`: Creates namespaced resolver for captured parameters in parent URLconf.\\n   - `_route_to_regex()`: Converts path() style routes to regex patterns, handling converters like <int:id>, <slug:name>, etc.\\n\\n3. **django/urls/base.py** - High-level URL routing API:\\n   - `resolve(path, urlconf=None)`: Entry point that resolves a URL path to a ResolverMatch object.\\n   - `reverse(viewname, urlconf=None, args=None, kwargs=None, current_app=None, query=None, fragment=None)`: Reverses a URL from a view name/path.\\n   - `reverse_lazy()`: Lazy version of reverse().\\n   - `is_valid_path()`: Convenience method to check if a path is valid.\\n   - `translate_url()`: Translates URLs for i18n.\\n   - `get_urlconf()`, `set_urlconf()`: Thread/task-local URLconf management.\\n   - `get_script_prefix()`, `set_script_prefix()`, `clear_script_prefix()`: SCRIPT_NAME prefix management.\\n   - `clear_url_caches()`: Clears cached resolvers and callables.\\n\\n4. **django/urls/converters.py** - Path converters for route parameters:\\n   - `IntConverter`, `StringConverter`, `UUIDConverter`, `SlugConverter`, `PathConverter`: Built-in converters for path() parameters.\\n   - `register_converter()`: Register custom converters.\\n   - `get_converters()`: Returns all available converters.\\n\\n5. **django/urls/utils.py** - Utility functions:\\n   - `get_callable(lookup_view)`: Resolves string view paths to callable functions.\\n   - `get_mod_func()`: Splits dotted paths into module and function parts.\\n\\n6. **django/urls/exceptions.py** - Exception classes:\\n   - `Resolver404`: Raised when URL resolution fails.\\n   - `NoReverseMatch`: Raised when URL reversal fails.\\n\\n7. **django/conf/urls/__init__.py** - Exports include and default error handlers.\\n\\n8. **django/conf/urls/i18n.py** - Internationalization support:\\n   - `i18n_patterns(*urls, prefix_default_language=True)`: Wraps URL patterns with language prefix.\\n   - `is_language_prefix_patterns_used()`: Detects if i18n_patterns is used.\\n\\n9. **django/conf/urls/static.py** - Debug static file serving:\\n   - `static(prefix, view=serve, **kwargs)`: Helper for serving media files in debug mode.\\n\\n10. **django/urls/__init__.py** - Main package that exports all public APIs.\\n\\n**Historical Note on patterns() function**: The `patterns()` function (used in Django versions before 1.10) has been removed and replaced with direct list-based urlpatterns. In the current codebase, URL patterns are defined as simple Python lists containing URLPattern and URLResolver objects created via path(), re_path(), and include() calls. The urlpatterns attribute is accessed and processed by include() and URLResolver.url_patterns property.\\n\\nThe current URL routing architecture processes both legacy patterns (through urlpatterns lists) and the modern routing through the common URLResolver, URLPattern, RegexPattern, and RoutePattern classes, with path converters providing type-safe parameter extraction.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}

The core files are:\\n\\n1. **django/urls/conf.py** - Provides the main URL configuration functions:\\n   - `include(arg, namespace=None)`: Includes another URL configuration, supporting tuples for namespace hints and app_name specification.\\n   - `path(route, view, kwargs=None, name=None)`: Modern path-based URL pattern using RoutePattern (replaces the deprecated Django 1.x url() function).\\n   - `re_path(route, view, kwargs=None, name=None)`: Regex-based URL pattern using RegexPattern (also replaces deprecated url()).\\n   - `_path()`: Internal function that both path() and re_path() are built from using functools.partial.\\n\\n2. **django/urls/resolvers.py** - Contains the URL dispatcher classes:\\n   - `URLResolver`: Main dispatcher class that resolves URLs to view callbacks, manages urlpatterns, and handles URL reversal. Has resolve() method for matching paths and _reverse_with_prefix() for URL reversal.\\n   - `URLPattern`: Represents a single URL pattern with a pattern object, callback view, default arguments, and name. Has resolve() method for matching.\\n   - `ResolverMatch`: Result object returned by URL resolution containing the matched view, args, kwargs, url_name, namespaces, and route information.\\n   - `RegexPattern`: Pattern class for regex-based URL patterns with LocaleRegexDescriptor for language-specific compilation.\\n   - `RoutePattern`: Pattern class for modern route-based URL patterns with converter support and LocaleRegexRouteDescriptor.\\n   - `LocalePrefixPattern`: Special pattern for i18n language prefix patterns.\\n   - `get_resolver(urlconf=None)`: Gets or creates a URLResolver instance with caching.\\n   - `get_ns_resolver()`: Creates namespaced resolver for captured parameters in parent URLconf.\\n   - `_route_to_regex()`: Converts path() style routes to regex patterns, handling converters like <int:id>, <slug:name>, etc.\\n\\n3. **django/urls/base.py** - High-level URL routing API:\\n   - `resolve(path, urlconf=None)`: Entry point that resolves a URL path to a ResolverMatch object.\\n   - `reverse(viewname, urlconf=None, args=None, kwargs=None, current_app=None, query=None, fragment=None)`: Reverses a URL from a view name/path.\\n   - `reverse_lazy()`: Lazy version of reverse().\\n   - `is_valid_path()`: Convenience method to check if a path is valid.\\n   - `translate_url()`: Translates URLs for i18n.\\n   - `get_urlconf()`, `set_urlconf()`: Thread/task-local URLconf management.\\n   - `get_script_prefix()`, `set_script_prefix()`, `clear_script_prefix()`: SCRIPT_NAME prefix management.\\n   - `clear_url_caches()`: Clears cached resolvers and callables.\\n\\n4. **django/urls/converters.py** - Path converters for route parameters:\\n   - `IntConverter`, `StringConverter`, `UUIDConverter`, `SlugConverter`, `PathConverter`: Built-in converters for path() parameters.\\n   - `register_converter()`: Register custom converters.\\n   - `get_converters()`: Returns all available converters.\\n\\n5. **django/urls/utils.py** - Utility functions:\\n   - `get_callable(lookup_view)`: Resolves string view paths to callable functions.\\n   - `get_mod_func()`: Splits dotted paths into module and function parts.\\n\\n6. **django/urls/exceptions.py** - Exception classes:\\n   - `Resolver404`: Raised when URL resolution fails.\\n   - `NoReverseMatch`: Raised when URL reversal fails.\\n\\n7. **django/conf/urls/__init__.py** - Exports include and default error handlers.\\n\\n8. **django/conf/urls/i18n.py** - Internationalization support:\\n   - `i18n_patterns(*urls, prefix_default_language=True)`: Wraps URL patterns with language prefix.\\n   - `is_language_prefix_patterns_used()`: Detects if i18n_patterns is used.\\n\\n9. **django/conf/urls/static.py** - Debug static file serving:\\n   - `static(prefix, view=serve, **kwargs)`: Helper for serving media files in debug mode.\\n\\n10. **django/urls/__init__.py** - Main package that exports all public APIs.\\n\\n**Historical Note on patterns() function**: The `patterns()` function (used in Django versions before 1.10) has been removed and replaced with direct list-based urlpatterns. In the current codebase, URL patterns are defined as simple Python lists containing URLPattern and URLResolver objects created via path(), re_path(), and include() calls. The urlpatterns attribute is accessed and processed by include() and URLResolver.url_patterns property.\\n\\nThe current URL routing architecture processes both legacy patterns (through urlpatterns lists) and the modern routing through the common URLResolver, URLPattern, RegexPattern, and RoutePattern classes, with path converters providing type-safe parameter extraction.\"\n}\n","numLines":69,"startLine":1,"totalLines":69}}}
